<rating>5</rating><name>Nick M<//name><date>1603342351507<//date>< text>
Great gym. Here's a waffle recipe:

Ingredients 250g Flour (plain)
7g Baking powder
20g Caster sugar
5g Salt
475ml Milk
2 Eggs
30ml Vegetable oil

Method

‚Ä¢Weigh all the dry ingredients, place in a large mixing bowl. Break the eggs into the milk and beat the mixture.

‚Ä¢Add the egg and milk mixture to the dry ingredients. Add the oil and mix all ingredients together until all the large lumps have been broken up. Do not over mix otherwise the waffles will be heavy when cooked.

‚Ä¢Pre heat the waffle maker and spray with oil (1 cal spray works well).

‚Ä¢Pour 3/4 of a cup of batter into the waffle maker and cook for 3-4 mins or until golden brown and crispy on the outside.

‚Ä¢Serve hot with maple syrup. Also good served with sliced banana or blueberries.

‚Ä¢Cooked waffles can be frozen and heated up in the toaster. Unused batter mixture can be kept in a container in the fridge for up to 2 days.<//text>

< Review>
In relation to the gyms around this area, this gym is absolutely PERFECT for me. The staff are nice and easy to talk to and ask questions and the weight floor is full of equipment! They have nearly a dozen benches that you can move around as you wish (compared to Cal Fam Fit which only has 4) and they are the ONLY place that I've found near Roseville that had more than 3 power racks (They have 5!). This place is for serious lifters and that was exactly the environment I wanted to find.

The people are nice and I've only had positive experiences with the people in my short 2 month membership of this gym. I could ask other members questions about equipment and they'd often be more than happy to help.

Sure this place doesn't have a sauna or a pool but they have absolutely everything that you need to change yourself for the better. If I find that i'm in need of a gym again down the line, I will be sure to pick this Gold's Gym over anything else in the area.<//Review>

<user_name>Monica< /user_name><date>1600382290953</date><rate>5< /rate><Text>I had an amazing experience visiting Rooky's for the first time. Upon arrival I was blown away by the mass qtys of 45s, which is what I came in looking for. I was warmly greeted by the owner, who asked me if I was looking for anything specific.
I was a bit overwhelmed by how much there was so him directing me to the area he thought I might best find what I wanted (he was right) I started digging!
Within the first 90 mims I had pulled at least 20 of interest, before having to run out and feed my meter. (You know it's a good dog when you have to feed your meter several times in one trip!)
Once I realized how long I had been in there I decided to stop digging and make my final selections. Besides the more expensive records for sale- all which were priced $5 or $10- there was also three times as many for sale priced at 3/$5.
After dbl checking my discogs where I have all my records I own inventoried (no more duplicate purchases- yay!) I narrowed my final selection down to 12 which I was super happy with. The best part was that four of them were ones on my wishlist!!
When I went to pay, the wonderful owner mentioned that I could bring him a wishlist and he'd be happy to see if he had any of them, which I thought was so great!
Besides how huge of a selection and the fair pricing, it was the kindness and helpfulness of the owner that really impressed me most. He was very sweet and genuinely wanted to help me and not just to make a quick sale. I mean this bc when I was about to pay, I asked him what Styrene meant. He explained the easiest way to tell and explained how vinyl esp motown would wear out over many plays, and suggested that I listen to a stevie wonder 45 I had in my hands just to be sure it was still in good playable cond. So he took me over to the turntables and showed me how to properly use it to  DBL check my selections, which I did. As a result, I put 3 of my 12 back. And even though he might have lost $5 on my total sale that day, his honesty and helpfulness will keep me coming back now again and again!
Overall it was a hugely positive 3 hour shopping experience, and I can't wait for my next dig!!< /Text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNPDPw_0PgaArmrj3keAMvanvLxLq2vYWaJqv0S=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMNmFuQaeeSY37NwCUVdB-Trq8gSyp3B4XZNZUm=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><resp>None</resp><gmapID>0x808580a134cefa15:0x65eafed9f8b13133< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>

<user_id>107760625157505589174<//user_id>< Name>
Stuart Fox</Name>
<time>1552759438382</time><rating>5< /rating>< text>
If you are looking for vinyl this is the place to go. On a typical day, if you're at the listening station, you'll see the oddest selection of the Buying and Selling vinyl cognoscenti slink in and out of the back room as they work their dark deals. Good news though: The scraps left behind by these apex predators are an eclectic and fascinating mix of old and new Soul, Funk, Gospel, Blues - Rock and Proto-Rock and at fair prices.  Somehow I ended up with the new Nick Waterhouse (Self Titled) LP - and it wasn't even available yet online.

Word of warning though - the proprietor is not a patient man and should be approached cautiously - he really knows his stuff, but if you walk in there in your favorite loafers and no socks - and start musing about how well 'curated' the place is, you are looking for trouble (as I learned).

When I saw that the local game in the back room is Cassino - I decided flex my card tactics to recover my honor. I was soundly put in my place there too -  but ended up with a nice branded felt slip mat for my trouble.< /text>

<Rate>1< /Rate><Review>Tried going there twice over the past week and wasn't open both times... just to give you context, I had to take the Caltrain to 22nd Street from Burlingame, and then take a pool cab or walk from the station to this record store. A plan like that is quite time consuming and requires clear planning.

But, despite me doing all of said planning, the store wasn't open on both occasions. Moreover, I went at 5.30PM the first time, and when I saw that it was closed, I thought 'Hey maybe they just shut shop a bit earlier today. That's alright... they have a life too'

But then I tried again a second time...this time at 3.00PM. After a long walk, mind you. I had planned my whole day around visiting this record store, in fact. But surprise surprise, it was closed. At 3 PM on a Thursday. Clearly they have their own personal interests ahead of business / customer service.

I'm thoroughly tired and disappointed.

I would NOT recommend that you go here unless you call ahead and confirm that it's open.

It seems to me, to be an operation run by real Rookies.< /Review><pictures>None<//pictures>< response>

<Text>My fiance and I love this place. The complex has great amenities like a nice clean gym, pool and club house that has foosball table and pool table. The apartment also comes with washer/dryer, refrigerator, stove, microwave and dishwasher. We have my moms dog once a month over for a weekend while she travels and we 've noticed that this complex is dog friendly which is a plus for dog lovers. They have free doggie waste bags and trash stations for it everywhere. This area of Chino Hills is lovely and it has a lot of different shopping centers and a mall near by. The complex is located right next to the 71 FWY so quick to get to the fwy.

I've seen bad reviews but honestly the only bad thing I can say is that the office management is very lazy sometimes, I've asked for simple questions before and they tell me they will get back to me and they never do. I always have to follow up and when I do they had already forgot about it. They are only quick when it comes to their convenience. For example this past February I forgot to make my payment on time because of the short month and I woke up the next day to an aggressive eviction notice. I knew it was my fault so I payed the late fee with no complaint but wow was that aggressive and I felt like, for being a A+ tenant I would get different treatment. I know at the end of the day that's their job but wanted to share this experience.

The good thing is that the maintenance management is great! You submit a request for maintenance and they come usually the same day to check it out and they are very friendly.

If you are a good tenant you should be fine with this complex. If you are a needy client and need constant communication with the office, you may find yourself very frustrated and upset.

Overall I love this place and been living here for 2 years but will unfortunately move out when my lease is over. The main reason is that I've notice the rent will go up every year and being a A+ tenant means nothing to them when in comes to negotiating last years rate. People have better chance at negotiation when dealing with smaller complexes.<//Text><GmapID>0x80dccd384729d617:0xeb57835ebce1770e<//GmapID>< Pictures>

The more popular and obvious locations are not as peaceful as it should. The location draws more folks who are looking for close attractions to the location. I would recommend using some of the other locations Motel 6 has. Many of the more secluded ones are more conducive to having a good nights rest and to not be disturbed. Went to one that was closer to common path and that has proven to be disruptive and didn't get a good nights rest. Overall, Motel 6 is practical and satisfactory.< /review>

Namu Williams<//user_name>
<Date>1505763505968</Date><rating>1<//rating>< Review>
The front desk staff were very friendly and accommodating, but that's where the good ends. The price was $113 for a Saturday night stay booked in advance - that's expensive for a motel, but super expensive for how dirty and uncomfortable this room was.

The room was neatly made up, but it had clearly not been cleaned properly. The floor was disgustingly dirty - we didn't realize just how bad it was until we took our shoes and socks off to shower (picture attached) - the hardwood floor felt like it hadn't been swept or mopped in months.

The shower was dirty, with hair in the drain and recent dirt stains (not the permanent kind, the kind you can wipe off with a rag). The towels had multiple stains and were so rough it was clear their usefulness as towels had long passed.

There was a roach under my son's bed - roaches don't bother me that much, but they really bothered my young son, who almost didn't want to sleep in the room any more. That was a hassle I definitely didn't want to deal with.

The parking lot had a lot of trash and debris and the pool area looked like it hadn't been cleaned in awhile.

Finally, they offered kids lollipops in the registration office, but I took a look at the container and the lollipops all looked like they had had their wrappers removed and then re-wrapped. One of them was put back in with no wrapper at all! (picture attached).

Overall, this Motel 6 is much dirtier and more uncomfortable to stay in that most Motel 6s I've been in, especially when you consider it's in San Luis Obispo, which is a beautiful town. Not worth the money. Spend another $20 or $30 and book at an actual hotel.</Review>

I had a wonderful stay at Motel 6 in San Luis Obispo (North); the amenities were basic but clean, and the rooms were serviced every day and kept very neat by the housekeeping staff.

< Review>
You don't expect much at a Motel 6 and you don't get much.  In our case, the shower enclosure had many long strands of black hair on the walls and floor and a partially used bar of soap in the shower.  Evidently it had not been cleaned since the last guest.  There were no shampoo or conditioner amenities either.  I don't know if Motel 6 is "bring your own" or if this too was an oversight by the housekeeping staff.  While the room seemed to have been recently painted, it and the bedding had that dank odor of stale cigarettes and I couldn't wear my pajamas when I got home the next night because they smelled of that room.  Our neighbors were very noisy, talking loudly right outside our door until very late and all of them were smokers, smoking outside their rooms all around us.  I saw a used hypodermic needle in the parking lot while walking the dog in the morning. (Good news, they allow pets which is a huge plus and the primary reason we stayed there).

It's not the Ritz but it's among the cheapest options around.</Review>
